# agents/co/core/elements/action_head.py
from __future__ import annotations
from typing import Any, Dict, Optional, List, Tuple
from collections import defaultdict
import random

# Optional translator/fuser; safe if absent
try:
    from agents.co.integration.translators import get_translator_for_family
except Exception:
    def get_translator_for_family(_fam: str):
        return None

try:
    from agents.co.core.combinators.C_fuse import C_Fuse
except Exception:
    class C_Fuse:  # type: ignore
        def __init__(self, method: str = "add", tau: float = 1.0): pass
        def fuse(self, scores_list: List[Dict[Any, float]]) -> Dict[Any, float]:
            out: Dict[Any, float] = {}
            for s in scores_list:
                for k, v in s.items():
                    out[k] = out.get(k, 0.0) + float(v)
            return out

try:
    from agents.co.core.contracts.signals import normalize_scores
except Exception:
    def normalize_scores(scores: Dict[Any, float]) -> Dict[Any, float]:
        if not scores:
            return {}
        m = max(abs(float(v)) for v in scores.values())
        if m <= 1e-12:
            return dict(scores)
        return {k: float(v) / m for k, v in scores.items()}

Coord = Tuple[int, int]

class ActionHead:
    """
    CO-first action head that can *blend* CO scores (bus + translator) with
    a small classical baseline, controlled by:
      - blend_mode: "mix" | "co_only" | "classic_only"
      - co_weight_override: float in [0,1] or None (then use header.state.co_weight)

    Returns dict:
      action, co_policy, co_bus_votes, co_weight, classic_weight, co_sources, head_eps, head_ngram_order
    """

    def __init__(
        self,
        seed: int = 0,
        # bandit
        eps_on_cycle: float = 0.10,
        # renewal (kept for API compatibility)
        ngram_order: int = 0,
        # maze
        greedy_explore_bias: float = 0.05,
        # fusion (for CO sources)
        fuse_method: str = "add",
        fuse_tau: float = 1.0,
        # routing knobs
        prefer_bus_if_present: bool = True,
        use_translator: bool = True,
        # BLEND knobs
        blend_mode: str = "mix",                 # "mix" | "co_only" | "classic_only"
        co_weight_override: Optional[float] = None,
    ) -> None:
        self.rng = random.Random(int(seed))
        self.eps = float(eps_on_cycle)
        self.k = max(0, int(ngram_order))
        self._maze_explore = float(greedy_explore_bias)
        self._fuser = C_Fuse(method=fuse_method, tau=fuse_tau)
        self.prefer_bus = bool(prefer_bus_if_present)
        self.use_translator = bool(use_translator)
        self.blend_mode = str(blend_mode)
        self.co_weight_override = co_weight_override

        # light bandit fallback state (only used if no primitive/translator/bus)
        self._counts: List[int] = []
        self._means: List[float] = []

    # ----------------- small helpers -----------------
    def _ensure_arms(self, n: int) -> None:
        while len(self._counts) < n:
            self._counts.append(0)
            self._means.append(0.0)

    def _default_action_space(self, family: str, observation: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[Any]:
        if family == "bandit":
            n_arms = int(observation.get("n_arms", 2))
            return list(range(n_arms))
        if family == "maze":
            return ["UP", "DOWN", "LEFT", "RIGHT"]
        if family == "renewal":
            A = int(observation.get("A", 0))
            return list(range(A)) if A > 0 else []
        return []

    def _bus_scores(self, primitives: Dict[str, Any], family: str) -> tuple[Dict[Any, float], int]:
        """Drain family votes from bus and aggregate weights per action."""
        bus = primitives.get("co_bus", None)
        if bus is None or not hasattr(bus, "drain"):
            return {}, 0
        try:
            votes = bus.drain(family)
        except Exception:
            votes = []
        agg: Dict[Any, float] = defaultdict(float)
        for v in votes:
            a = v.get("action", None)
            w = float(v.get("weight", 0.0) or 0.0)
            if a is not None and w > 0.0:
                agg[a] += w
        return dict(agg), len(votes)

    def _classical_scores(self, family: str, obs: Dict[str, Any], primitives: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[Any, float]:
        """
        Minimal classical baselines:
          - bandit: empirical means via primitive bandit_stats (else internal)
          - renewal: predict-last
          - maze: greedy-to-goal (non-improving moves get a small floor)
        """
        if family == "bandit":
            n = int(obs.get("n_arms", 2))
            bs = primitives.get("bandit_stats")
            if bs is not None and all(hasattr(bs, k) for k in ("ensure","means","counts")):
                try:
                    bs.ensure(n)
                    means = list(bs.means[:n])
                except Exception:
                    self._ensure_arms(n); means = list(self._means[:n])
            else:
                self._ensure_arms(n); means = list(self._means[:n])
            if any(means):
                lo, hi = min(means), max(means)
                rng = (hi - lo) if (hi > lo) else 1.0
                return {i: (means[i]-lo)/rng for i in range(n)}
            return {i: 0.0 for i in range(n)}

        if family == "renewal":
            a = int(obs.get("obs", 0))
            return {a: 1.0}

        if family == "maze":
            pos = obs.get("pos"); goal = obs.get("goal")
            H = obs.get("height"); W = obs.get("width"); grid = obs.get("grid")
            if not (isinstance(pos,(list,tuple)) and isinstance(goal,(list,tuple))):
                return {}
            pr,pc = int(pos[0]), int(pos[1]); gr,gc = int(goal[0]), int(goal[1])
            dirs = ("UP","DOWN","LEFT","RIGHT")
            deltas = {"UP":(-1,0),"DOWN":(1,0),"LEFT":(0,-1),"RIGHT":(0,1)}
            def inb(r,c):
                if H is None or W is None: return True
                try: return 0 <= r < int(H) and 0 <= c < int(W)
                except Exception: return True
            def free(r,c):
                if not inb(r,c): return False
                if grid is None: return True
                try: return int(grid[r][c]) == 0
                except Exception: return True
            d0 = abs(pr-gr)+abs(pc-gc)
            scores: Dict[str, float] = {}
            for d in dirs:
                dr,dc = deltas[d]; nr,nc = pr+dr, pc+dc
                if not free(nr,nc):
                    continue
                d1 = abs(nr-gr)+abs(nc-gc)
                improve = d0 - d1
                scores[d] = 1.0 if (improve > 0.0) else 0.2
            return scores

        return {}

    # ----------------- hooks -----------------
    def update(
        self,
        observation: Dict[str, Any],
        primitives: Dict[str, Any],
        header: Any,
        feedback: Optional[Dict[str, Any]],
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        fam = str(observation.get("family", "")).lower()

        # fallback bandit stats update only when no primitive
        if fam == "bandit" and isinstance(feedback, dict):
            a = feedback.get("action", None)
            r = feedback.get("reward", None)
            n_arms = int(observation.get("n_arms", 2))
            bs = primitives.get("bandit_stats")
            if isinstance(a, int) and isinstance(r, (int, float)):
                if bs is not None and hasattr(bs, "update"):
                    try:
                        bs.update(int(a), float(r), n_arms=n_arms)
                    except Exception:
                        self._ensure_arms(n_arms)
                        self._counts[a] += 1
                        n = max(1, self._counts[a])
                        self._means[a] += (float(r) - self._means[a]) / float(n)
                else:
                    self._ensure_arms(n_arms)
                    self._counts[a] += 1
                    n = max(1, self._counts[a])
                    self._means[a] += (float(r) - self._means[a]) / float(n)
        return {}

    def step(
        self,
        observation: Dict[str, Any],
        primitives: Dict[str, Any],
        header: Any,
        feedback: Optional[Dict[str, Any]],
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            family = str(observation.get("family", "")).lower()
            actions = observation.get("action_space") or self._default_action_space(family, observation)

            # --- weights ---
            if self.co_weight_override is not None:
                co_w = float(max(0.0, min(1.0, self.co_weight_override)))
            else:
                try:
                    co_w = float(getattr(header, "state", {}).get("co_weight", 1.0))
                except Exception:
                    co_w = 1.0
            if self.blend_mode == "co_only":
                co_w = 1.0
            elif self.blend_mode == "classic_only":
                co_w = 0.0
            classic_w = 1.0 - co_w

            # --- CO path (bus, then translator, then fuse) ---
            co_sources: List[str] = []
            bus_scores, n_votes = ({}, 0)
            if self.prefer_bus:
                bus_scores, n_votes = self._bus_scores(primitives, family)
                if bus_scores:
                    co_sources.append("bus")

            trans_scores = {}
            translator_mask: set = set()
            if self.use_translator:
                translator = get_translator_for_family(family)
                if translator is not None:
                    tcfg = {
                        "eps": self.eps,
                        "maze_explore": self._maze_explore,
                        "k": self.k,
                    }
                    try:
                        trans_scores, translator_mask, _info = translator(observation, header, primitives, {}, tcfg)
                    except Exception:
                        trans_scores, translator_mask = {}, set()
                    if trans_scores:
                        co_sources.append("translator")

            co_scores = {}
            parts = []
            if bus_scores:   parts.append(bus_scores)
            if trans_scores: parts.append(trans_scores)
            if parts:
                co_scores = self._fuser.fuse(parts)
                co_scores = normalize_scores(co_scores)
            # apply translator mask to CO scores (if any)
            for a in list(co_scores.keys()):
                if a in translator_mask:
                    co_scores.pop(a, None)

            

            # --- classical path ---
            classical = self._classical_scores(family, observation, primitives)
            if classical:
                classical = normalize_scores(classical)
                co_sources.append("classical")  # we will blend it (possibly with weight 0)

            # --- assemble final scores ---
            domain = list(actions) if actions else list(set(list(co_scores.keys()) + list(classical.keys())))
            final_scores: Dict[Any, float] = {}
            if domain:
                for a in domain:
                    cs = co_scores.get(a, 0.0)
                    ks = classical.get(a, 0.0)
                    final_scores[a] = co_w * cs + classic_w * ks
                
            if final_scores:
                best = max(final_scores, key=final_scores.get)
                return {
                    "action": best,
                    "co_policy": f"{family}:blend(co={co_w:.2f})",
                    "co_bus_votes": int(n_votes),
                    "co_weight": float(co_w),
                    "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                    "co_sources": co_sources,
                    "head_eps": float(self.eps),
                    "head_ngram_order": int(self.k),
                }

            # -------- HEURISTIC FALLBACKS --------------------
            if family == "bandit":
                n_arms = int(observation.get("n_arms", 2))
                self._ensure_arms(n_arms)
                for i in range(n_arms):
                    if self._counts[i] == 0:
                        return {"action": i, "co_policy": "bandit:fallback_roundrobin",
                                "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_weight": float(co_w), "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                                "co_sources": ["fallback"], "head_eps": float(self.eps), "head_ngram_order": int(self.k)}
                if self.rng.random() < self.eps:
                    a = self.rng.randrange(n_arms)
                else:
                    a = max(range(n_arms), key=lambda j: self._means[j])
                return {"action": a, "co_policy": "bandit:fallback_egreedy",
                        "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_weight": float(co_w), "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                        "co_sources": ["fallback"], "head_eps": float(self.eps), "head_ngram_order": int(self.k)}

            if family == "renewal":
                a = int(observation.get("obs", 0))
                return {"action": a, "co_policy": "renewal:fallback_predict_last",
                        "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_weight": float(co_w), "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                        "co_sources": ["fallback"], "head_eps": float(self.eps), "head_ngram_order": int(self.k)}

            if family == "maze":
                pos = observation.get("pos"); goal = observation.get("goal")
                if isinstance(pos, (list, tuple)) and isinstance(goal, (list, tuple)):
                    pr, pc = int(pos[0]), int(pos[1])
                    gr, gc = int(goal[0]), int(goal[1])
                    dirs = ("UP", "DOWN", "LEFT", "RIGHT")
                    deltas = {"UP": (-1, 0), "DOWN": (1, 0), "LEFT": (0, -1), "RIGHT": (0, 1)}
                    best = None; best_improve = -1e9
                    d0 = abs(pr - gr) + abs(pc - gc)
                    for d in dirs:
                        dr, dc = deltas[d]
                        d1 = abs((pr + dr) - gr) + abs((pc + dc) - gc)
                        improve = d0 - d1
                        if improve > best_improve:
                            best_improve = improve
                            best = d
                    return {"action": best or "RIGHT", "co_policy": "maze:fallback_greedy",
                            "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_weight": float(co_w), "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                            "co_sources": ["fallback"], "head_eps": float(self.eps), "head_ngram_order": int(self.k)}

            # Unknown family or no choice available
            if actions:
                return {"action": actions[0], "co_policy": "fallback:any",
                        "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_weight": float(co_w), "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                        "co_sources": ["fallback"], "head_eps": float(self.eps), "head_ngram_order": int(self.k)}
            return {}

        except Exception:
            # Ultra-robust maze fallback so the runner never stalls
            fam = str(observation.get("family","")).lower()
            if fam == "maze":
                pos = observation.get("pos"); goal = observation.get("goal")
                if isinstance(pos,(list,tuple)) and isinstance(goal,(list,tuple)):
                    pr, pc = int(pos[0]), int(pos[1]); gr, gc = int(goal[0]), int(goal[1])
                    dirs = ("UP","DOWN","LEFT","RIGHT")
                    deltas = {"UP":(-1,0),"DOWN":(1,0),"LEFT":(0,-1),"RIGHT":(0,1)}
                    best = None; best_improve = -1e9
                    d0 = abs(pr-gr)+abs(pc-gc)
                    for d in dirs:
                        dr,dc = deltas[d]
                        d1 = abs(pr+dr-gr)+abs(pc+dc-gc)
                        imp = d0 - d1
                        if imp > best_improve:
                            best_improve, best = imp, d
                    return {"action": best or "RIGHT", "co_policy": "maze:fallback_greedy", "co_bus_votes": 0,
                            "co_sources": ["fallback"]}
            # unknown family: pick anything
            actions = observation.get("action_space") or []
            return {"action": (actions[0] if actions else None), "co_policy": "fallback:any",
                    "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_sources": ["fallback"]}

    def run_update(
        self,
        elements: list,
        primitives: dict,
        header: any,
        observation: dict,
        feedback: dict | None,
    ) -> dict:
        """Learning-only pass; no ActionHead.step, no return of an action."""
        out: dict = {}
        try:
            hrec = header.update(observation)
            if isinstance(hrec, dict):
                out.update(hrec)
        except Exception:
            pass

        for e in elements:
            # skip ActionHead entirely on update pass
            if e.__class__.__name__.lower().endswith("actionhead"):
                continue

            if hasattr(e, "update"):
                try:
                    u = e.update(observation, primitives, header, feedback)
                    if isinstance(u, dict) and u:
                        out.update(u)
                except Exception:
                    pass

            if hasattr(e, "step"):
                try:
                    s = e.step(observation, primitives, header, feedback)
                    if isinstance(s, dict) and s:
                        out.update(s)
                except Exception:
                    pass

            if hasattr(e, "metrics"):
                try:
                    m = e.metrics()
                    if isinstance(m, dict) and m:
                        out.update(m)
                except Exception:
                    pass

        return out

    def metrics(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "head_eps": float(self.eps),
            "head_ngram_order": int(self.k),
        }


and

# agents/co/core/combinators/C_pipeline.py

from __future__ import annotations

from typing import Any, Dict, List

from agents.co.core.contracts.signals import merge_signals


class C_Pipeline:

    """

    Executes elements in sequence; each element may expose: update/step/metrics.

    Builds a 'co_bus' (namespaced signals) so later elements (e.g., ActionHead)

    can read all previously published signals via header.state["co_bus"].

    """


    def __init__(self, order: List[str] | None = None):

        self.order = order or []


    # agents/co/core/combinators/C_pipeline.py  (run method)


    def run(

        self,

        elements: list,

        primitives: dict,

        header: any,

        observation: dict,

        feedback: dict | None,

    ) -> dict:

        """

        Single-pass decision pipeline:

        1) header.update(observation)

        2) run elements.update(), then elements.step() for all *non-ActionHead* elements

        3) run ActionHead.step() once (last) and return its dict (plus any merged metrics)

        """

        out: dict = {}


        # 0) Ensure header is updated so ActionHead can read co_weight/dyn

        try:

            hrec = header.update(observation)

            if isinstance(hrec, dict):

                out.update(hrec)

        except Exception:

            pass


        # 1) Walk elements: everything except ActionHead first

        head = None

        for e in elements:

            if e.__class__.__name__.lower().endswith("actionhead"):

                head = e

                continue


            # optional update

            if hasattr(e, "update"):

                try:

                    u = e.update(observation, primitives, header, feedback)

                    if isinstance(u, dict) and u:

                        out.update(u)

                except Exception:

                    pass


            # main step

            if hasattr(e, "step"):

                try:

                    s = e.step(observation, primitives, header, feedback)

                    if isinstance(s, dict) and s:

                        out.update(s)

                except Exception:

                    pass


            # optional metrics

            if hasattr(e, "metrics"):

                try:

                    m = e.metrics()

                    if isinstance(m, dict) and m:

                        out.update(m)

                except Exception:

                    pass


        # 2) ActionHead exactly once, last

        if head is not None and hasattr(head, "step"):

            try:

                sel = head.step(observation, primitives, header, feedback)

                if isinstance(sel, dict) and sel:

                    out.update(sel)

                    return out  # <-- RETURN immediately with the decision

            except Exception:

                pass


        # 3) Fallback if no head or head returned nothing

        return out

#ChangeOntCode\agents\co\adapters\maze_adapter.py

from __future__ import annotations

from typing import Any, Dict, Optional


class COAdapterMaze:

    def __init__(self, core, name: str = "CO") -> None:

        self.core = core

        self.name = name

        self._head = None

        self._bridge = None

        for e in getattr(core, "elements", []):

            nm = e.__class__.__name__.lower()

            if nm == "actionhead":

                self._head = e

            if nm == "e0_votebridge":

                self._bridge = e


    def _ensure_bus(self) -> None:

        if "co_bus" not in self.core.primitives:

            try:

                from agents.co.core.primitives.co_bus import CoVoteBus

                self.core.primitives["co_bus"] = CoVoteBus()

            except Exception:

                # tiny inline bus

                class _Bus:

                    def __init__(self): self._s = {}

                    def push(self,f,a,weight=1.0,**kw):

                        self._s.setdefault(f,[]).append({"action":a,"weight":float(weight),**kw})

                    def drain(self,f): lst=self._s.get(f,[]); self._s[f]=[]; return lst

                    def peek(self,f):  return list(self._s.get(f,[]))

                    def size(self,f):  return len(self._s.get(f,[]))

                self.core.primitives["co_bus"] = _Bus()


    def select(self, observation: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        obs = dict(observation or {})

        obs.setdefault("family", "maze")


        # 1) header update (publishes co_weight etc.)

        hdr = {}

        try:

            hdr = self.core.header.update(obs) or {}

        except Exception:

            pass


        # 2) ensure bus exists

        self._ensure_bus()


        # 3) PRIME the bus explicitly via vote_bridge

        if self._bridge is not None:

            try:

                self._bridge.step(obs, self.core.primitives, self.core.header, None)

            except Exception:

                pass


        # 4) HEAD decides (translator/bus/fallback logic is inside the head)

        out: Dict[str, Any] = {}

        if self._head is not None:

            try:

                out = self._head.step(obs, self.core.primitives, self.core.header, None) or {}

            except Exception:

                out = {}


        # 5) merge telemetry and apply a last safety guard

        merged = {**hdr, **(out if isinstance(out, dict) else {})}

        act = merged.get("action")

        if act not in ("UP", "DOWN", "LEFT", "RIGHT"):

            merged["action"] = "RIGHT"

            merged.setdefault("co_policy", "maze:safe_default")

            merged.setdefault("co_bus_votes", 0)

        return merged


    def update(self, feedback: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:

        # lightweight per-step updates (bandit stats etc.)

        try:

            self.core.combinators["pipeline"].run(

                self.core.elements, self.core.primitives, self.core.header,

                {"family": "maze"}, feedback or {}

            )

        except Exception:

            pass

#ChangeOntCode\agents\co\adapters\bandit_adapter.py

from __future__ import annotations

from typing import Any, Dict


class COAdapterBandit:

    def __init__(self, core, name: str = "CO", n_arms: int = 2) -> None:

        self.core = core

        self.name = name

        self.n_arms = int(n_arms)

        self._head = None

        self._bridge = None

        for e in getattr(core, "elements", []):

            nm = e.__class__.__name__.lower()

            if nm == "actionhead":     self._head = e

            if nm == "e0_votebridge":  self._bridge = e


    def _ensure_bus(self) -> None:

        if "co_bus" not in self.core.primitives:

            try:

                from agents.co.core.primitives.co_bus import CoVoteBus

                self.core.primitives["co_bus"] = CoVoteBus()

            except Exception:

                pass


    def select(self, observation: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        obs = dict(observation or {})

        obs.setdefault("family", "bandit")

        obs.setdefault("n_arms", self.n_arms)


        hdr = {}

        try:

            hdr = self.core.header.update(obs) or {}

        except Exception:

            pass


        self._ensure_bus()


        # prime bus with bridge

        if self._bridge is not None:

            try:

                self._bridge.step(obs, self.core.primitives, self.core.header, None)

            except Exception:

                pass


        # head decides

        out: Dict[str, Any] = {}

        if self._head is not None:

            try:

                out = self._head.step(obs, self.core.primitives, self.core.header, None) or {}

            except Exception:

                out = {}


        merged = {**hdr, **(out if isinstance(out, dict) else {})}

        if "action" not in merged or not isinstance(merged["action"], int):

            merged["action"] = 0

            merged.setdefault("co_policy", "bandit:safe_default")

            merged.setdefault("co_bus_votes", 0)

        return merged


    def update(self, feedback: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:

        try:

            self.core.combinators["pipeline"].run(

                self.core.elements, self.core.primitives, self.core.header,

                {"family": "bandit", "n_arms": self.n_arms}, feedback or {}

            )

        except Exception:

            pass

#ChangeOntCode\agents\co\adapters\renewal_adapter.py

from __future__ import annotations

from typing import Any, Dict


class COAdapterRenewal:

    def __init__(self, core, name: str = "CO") -> None:

        self.core = core

        self.name = name

        self._head = None

        self._bridge = None

        for e in getattr(core, "elements", []):

            nm = e.__class__.__name__.lower()

            if nm == "actionhead":     self._head = e

            if nm == "e0_votebridge":  self._bridge = e


    def _ensure_bus(self) -> None:

        if "co_bus" not in self.core.primitives:

            try:

                from agents.co.core.primitives.co_bus import CoVoteBus

                self.core.primitives["co_bus"] = CoVoteBus()

            except Exception:

                pass


    def select(self, observation: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        obs = dict(observation or {})

        obs.setdefault("family", "renewal")


        hdr = {}

        try:

            hdr = self.core.header.update(obs) or {}

        except Exception:

            pass


        self._ensure_bus()


        # prime bus with bridge

        if self._bridge is not None:

            try:

                self._bridge.step(obs, self.core.primitives, self.core.header, None)

            except Exception:

                pass


        # head decides

        out: Dict[str, Any] = {}

        if self._head is not None:

            try:

                out = self._head.step(obs, self.core.primitives, self.core.header, None) or {}

            except Exception:

                out = {}


        merged = {**hdr, **(out if isinstance(out, dict) else {})}

        if "action" not in merged:

            merged["action"] = int(obs.get("obs", 0))

            merged.setdefault("co_policy", "renewal:safe_default")

            merged.setdefault("co_bus_votes", 0)

        return merged


    def update(self, feedback: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:

        try:

            self.core.combinators["pipeline"].run(

                self.core.elements, self.core.primitives, self.core.header,

                {"family": "renewal"}, feedback or {}

            )

        except Exception:

            pass

def step(
        self,
        observation: Dict[str, Any],
        primitives: Dict[str, Any],
        header: Any,
        feedback: Optional[Dict[str, Any]],
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            family = str(observation.get("family", "")).lower()
            actions = observation.get("action_space") or self._default_action_space(family, observation)
            # --- weights ---
            if self.co_weight_override is not None:
                co_w = float(max(0.0, min(1.0, self.co_weight_override)))
            else:
                try:
                    co_w = float(getattr(header, "state", {}).get("co_weight", 1.0))
                except Exception:
                    co_w = 1.0
            if self.blend_mode == "co_only":
                co_w = 1.0
            elif self.blend_mode == "classic_only":
                co_w = 0.0
            classic_w = 1.0 - co_w
            # --- CO path (bus, then translator, then fuse) ---
            co_sources: List[str] = []
            bus_scores, n_votes = ({}, 0)
            if self.prefer_bus:
                bus_scores, n_votes = self._bus_scores(primitives, family)
                if bus_scores:
                    co_sources.append("bus")
            trans_scores = {}
            translator_mask: set = set()
            if self.use_translator:
                translator = get_translator_for_family(family)
                if translator is not None:
                    tcfg = {
                        "eps": self.eps,
                        "maze_explore": self._maze_explore,
                        "k": self.k,
                    }
                    try:
                        trans_scores, translator_mask, _info = translator(observation, header, primitives, {}, tcfg)
                    except Exception:
                        trans_scores, translator_mask = {}, set()
                    if trans_scores:
                        co_sources.append("translator")
            co_scores = {}
            parts = []
            if bus_scores:   parts.append(bus_scores)
            if trans_scores: parts.append(trans_scores)
            if parts:
                co_scores = self._fuser.fuse(parts)
                co_scores = normalize_scores(co_scores)
            # apply translator mask to CO scores (if any)
            for a in list(co_scores.keys()):
                if a in translator_mask:
                    co_scores.pop(a, None)
            
            # --- classical path ---
            classical = self._classical_scores(family, observation, primitives)
            if classical:
                classical = normalize_scores(classical)
                co_sources.append("classical")  # we will blend it (possibly with weight 0)
            # --- assemble final scores ---
            domain = list(actions) if actions else list(set(list(co_scores.keys()) + list(classical.keys())))
            final_scores: Dict[Any, float] = {}
            if domain:
                for a in domain:
                    cs = co_scores.get(a, 0.0)
                    ks = classical.get(a, 0.0)
                    final_scores[a] = co_w * cs + classic_w * ks
                
            if final_scores:
                best = max(final_scores, key=final_scores.get)
                return {
                    "action": best,
                    "co_policy": f"{family}:blend(co={co_w:.2f})",
                    "co_bus_votes": int(n_votes),
                    "co_weight": float(co_w),
                    "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                    "co_sources": co_sources,
                    "head_eps": float(self.eps),
                    "head_ngram_order": int(self.k),
                }
            # -------- HEURISTIC FALLBACKS --------------------
            if family == "bandit":
                n_arms = int(observation.get("n_arms", 2))
                self._ensure_arms(n_arms)
                for i in range(n_arms):
                    if self._counts[i] == 0:
                        return {"action": i, "co_policy": "bandit:fallback_roundrobin",
                                "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_weight": float(co_w), "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                                "co_sources": ["fallback"], "head_eps": float(self.eps), "head_ngram_order": int(self.k)}
                if self.rng.random() < self.eps:
                    a = self.rng.randrange(n_arms)
                else:
                    a = max(range(n_arms), key=lambda j: self._means[j])
                return {"action": a, "co_policy": "bandit:fallback_egreedy",
                        "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_weight": float(co_w), "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                        "co_sources": ["fallback"], "head_eps": float(self.eps), "head_ngram_order": int(self.k)}
            if family == "renewal":
                a = int(observation.get("obs", 0))
                return {"action": a, "co_policy": "renewal:fallback_predict_last",
                        "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_weight": float(co_w), "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                        "co_sources": ["fallback"], "head_eps": float(self.eps), "head_ngram_order": int(self.k)}
            if family == "maze":
                pos = observation.get("pos"); goal = observation.get("goal")
                if isinstance(pos, (list, tuple)) and isinstance(goal, (list, tuple)):
                    pr, pc = int(pos[0]), int(pos[1])
                    gr, gc = int(goal[0]), int(goal[1])
                    dirs = ("UP", "DOWN", "LEFT", "RIGHT")
                    deltas = {"UP": (-1, 0), "DOWN": (1, 0), "LEFT": (0, -1), "RIGHT": (0, 1)}
                    best = None; best_improve = -1e9
                    d0 = abs(pr - gr) + abs(pc - gc)
                    for d in dirs:
                        dr, dc = deltas[d]
                        d1 = abs((pr + dr) - gr) + abs((pc + dc) - gc)
                        improve = d0 - d1
                        if improve > best_improve:
                            best_improve = improve
                            best = d
                    return {"action": best or "RIGHT", "co_policy": "maze:fallback_greedy",
                            "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_weight": float(co_w), "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                            "co_sources": ["fallback"], "head_eps": float(self.eps), "head_ngram_order": int(self.k)}
            # Unknown family or no choice available
            if actions:
                return {"action": actions[0], "co_policy": "fallback:any",
                        "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_weight": float(co_w), "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                        "co_sources": ["fallback"], "head_eps": float(self.eps), "head_ngram_order": int(self.k)}
            return {}
        except Exception:
            # Ultra-robust maze fallback so the runner never stalls
            fam = str(observation.get("family","")).lower()
            if fam == "maze":
                pos = observation.get("pos"); goal = observation.get("goal")
                if isinstance(pos,(list,tuple)) and isinstance(goal,(list,tuple)):
                    pr, pc = int(pos[0]), int(pos[1]); gr, gc = int(goal[0]), int(goal[1])
                    dirs = ("UP","DOWN","LEFT","RIGHT")
                    deltas = {"UP":(-1,0),"DOWN":(1,0),"LEFT":(0,-1),"RIGHT":(0,1)}
                    best = None; best_improve = -1e9
                    d0 = abs(pr-gr)+abs(pc-gc)
                    for d in dirs:
                        dr,dc = deltas[d]
                        d1 = abs(pr+dr-gr)+abs(pc+dc-gc)
                        imp = d0 - d1
                        if imp > best_improve:
                            best_improve, best = imp, d
                    return {"action": best or "RIGHT", "co_policy": "maze:fallback_greedy", "co_bus_votes": 0,
                            "co_sources": ["fallback"]}
            # unknown family: pick anything
            actions = observation.get("action_space") or []
            return {"action": (actions[0] if actions else None), "co_policy": "fallback:any",
                    "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_sources": ["fallback"]}
    def run_update(
        self,
        elements: list,
        primitives: dict,
        header: any,
        observation: dict,
        feedback: dict | None,
    ) -> dict:
        """Learning-only pass; no ActionHead.step, no return of an action."""
        out: dict = {}
        try:
            hrec = header.update(observation)
            if isinstance(hrec, dict):
                out.update(hrec)
        except Exception:
            pass
        for e in elements:
            # skip ActionHead entirely on update pass
            if e.__class__.__name__.lower().endswith("actionhead"):
                continue
            if hasattr(e, "update"):
                try:
                    u = e.update(observation, primitives, header, feedback)
                    if isinstance(u, dict) and u:
                        out.update(u)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            if hasattr(e, "step"):
                try:
                    s = e.step(observation, primitives, header, feedback)
                    if isinstance(s, dict) and s:
                        out.update(s)
                except Exception:
                    pass
            if hasattr(e, "metrics"):
                try:
                    m = e.metrics()
                    if isinstance(m, dict) and m:
                        out.update(m)
                except Exception:
                    pass
        return out
    def metrics(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "head_eps": float(self.eps),
            "head_ngram_order": int(self.k),
        }
this:


def _classical_scores(self, family: str, obs: Dict[str, Any], primitives: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[Any, float]:

        """

        Minimal classical baselines:

          - bandit: empirical means via primitive bandit_stats (else internal)

          - renewal: predict-last

          - maze: greedy-to-goal (non-improving moves get a small floor)

        """

        if family == "bandit":

            n = int(obs.get("n_arms", 2))

            bs = primitives.get("bandit_stats")

            if bs is not None and all(hasattr(bs, k) for k in ("ensure","means","counts")):

                try:

                    bs.ensure(n)

                    means = list(bs.means[:n])

                except Exception:

                    self._ensure_arms(n); means = list(self._means[:n])

            else:

                self._ensure_arms(n); means = list(self._means[:n])

            if any(means):

                lo, hi = min(means), max(means)

                rng = (hi - lo) if (hi > lo) else 1.0

                return {i: (means[i]-lo)/rng for i in range(n)}

            return {i: 0.0 for i in range(n)}


        if family == "renewal":

            a = int(obs.get("obs", 0))

            return {a: 1.0}


        if family == "maze":

            pos = obs.get("pos"); goal = obs.get("goal")

            H = obs.get("height"); W = obs.get("width"); grid = obs.get("grid")


            if not (isinstance(pos,(list,tuple)) and isinstance(goal,(list,tuple))):

                print("[CLASSIC] missing pos/goal -> no classical scores")

                return {}


            pr,pc = int(pos[0]), int(pos[1]); gr,gc = int(goal[0]), int(goal[1])

            dirs = ("UP","DOWN","LEFT","RIGHT")

            deltas = {"UP":(-1,0),"DOWN":(1,0),"LEFT":(0,-1),"RIGHT":(0,1)}


            def inb(r,c):

                if H is None or W is None: return True

                try: return 0 <= r < int(H) and 0 <= c < int(W)

                except Exception: return True


            def free(r,c):

                if not inb(r,c): return False

                if grid is None: return True

                try: return int(grid[r][c]) == 0

                except Exception: return True


            print(f"[CLASSIC] pos={ (pr,pc) } goal={ (gr,gc) } HxW={H}x{W} grid_is_list={ isinstance(grid, list) }")


            d0 = abs(pr-gr)+abs(pc-gc)

            scores: Dict[str, float] = {}


            for d,(dr,dc) in deltas.items():

                nr, nc = pr+dr, pc+dc

                ok = free(nr,nc)

                cell = None

                if isinstance(grid, list) and H is not None and W is not None and 0 <= nr < int(H) and 0 <= nc < int(W):

                    try:

                        cell = int(grid[nr][nc])

                    except Exception:

                        cell = "?"


                print(f"[CLASSIC] dir={d} -> next={(nr,nc)} free={ok} cell={cell}")


                if not ok:

                    continue


                d1 = abs(nr-gr)+abs(nc-gc)

                improve = d0 - d1

                scores[d] = 1.0 if (improve > 0.0) else 0.2


            print("[CLASSIC] scores=", scores)

            return scores


        return {}

# agents/co/core/elements/action_head.py
from __future__ import annotations
from typing import Any, Dict, Optional, List, Tuple
from collections import defaultdict
import random

# Optional translator/fuser; safe if absent
try:
    from agents.co.integration.translators import get_translator_for_family
except Exception:
    def get_translator_for_family(_fam: str):
        return None

try:
    from agents.co.core.combinators.C_fuse import C_Fuse
except Exception:
    class C_Fuse:  # type: ignore
        def __init__(self, method: str = "add", tau: float = 1.0): pass
        def fuse(self, scores_list: List[Dict[Any, float]]) -> Dict[Any, float]:
            out: Dict[Any, float] = {}
            for s in scores_list:
                for k, v in s.items():
                    out[k] = out.get(k, 0.0) + float(v)
            return out

try:
    from agents.co.core.contracts.signals import normalize_scores
except Exception:
    def normalize_scores(scores: Dict[Any, float]) -> Dict[Any, float]:
        if not scores:
            return {}
        m = max(abs(float(v)) for v in scores.values())
        if m <= 1e-12:
            return dict(scores)
        return {k: float(v) / m for k, v in scores.items()}

Coord = Tuple[int, int]

class ActionHead:
    """
    CO-first action head that can *blend* CO scores (bus + translator) with
    a small classical baseline, controlled by:
      - blend_mode: "mix" | "co_only" | "classic_only"
      - co_weight_override: float in [0,1] or None (then use header.state.co_weight)

    Returns dict:
      action, co_policy, co_bus_votes, co_weight, classic_weight, co_sources, head_eps, head_ngram_order
    """

    def __init__(
        self,
        seed: int = 0,
        # bandit
        eps_on_cycle: float = 0.10,
        # renewal (kept for API compatibility)
        ngram_order: int = 0,
        # maze
        greedy_explore_bias: float = 0.05,
        # fusion (for CO sources)
        fuse_method: str = "add",
        fuse_tau: float = 1.0,
        # routing knobs
        prefer_bus_if_present: bool = True,
        use_translator: bool = True,
        # BLEND knobs
        blend_mode: str = "mix",                 # "mix" | "co_only" | "classic_only"
        co_weight_override: Optional[float] = None,
    ) -> None:
        self.rng = random.Random(int(seed))
        self.eps = float(eps_on_cycle)
        self.k = max(0, int(ngram_order))
        self._maze_explore = float(greedy_explore_bias)
        self._fuser = C_Fuse(method=fuse_method, tau=fuse_tau)
        self.prefer_bus = bool(prefer_bus_if_present)
        self.use_translator = bool(use_translator)
        self.blend_mode = str(blend_mode)
        self.co_weight_override = co_weight_override

        # light bandit fallback state (only used if no primitive/translator/bus)
        self._counts: List[int] = []
        self._means: List[float] = []

    # ----------------- small helpers -----------------
    def _ensure_arms(self, n: int) -> None:
        while len(self._counts) < n:
            self._counts.append(0)
            self._means.append(0.0)

    def _default_action_space(self, family: str, observation: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[Any]:
        if family == "bandit":
            n_arms = int(observation.get("n_arms", 2))
            return list(range(n_arms))
        if family == "maze":
            return ["UP", "DOWN", "LEFT", "RIGHT"]
        if family == "renewal":
            A = int(observation.get("A", 0))
            return list(range(A)) if A > 0 else []
        return []

    def _bus_scores(self, primitives: Dict[str, Any], family: str) -> tuple[Dict[Any, float], int]:
        """Drain family votes from bus and aggregate weights per action."""
        bus = primitives.get("co_bus", None)
        if bus is None or not hasattr(bus, "drain"):
            return {}, 0
        try:
            votes = bus.drain(family)
        except Exception:
            votes = []
        agg: Dict[Any, float] = defaultdict(float)
        for v in votes:
            a = v.get("action", None)
            w = float(v.get("weight", 0.0) or 0.0)
            if a is not None and w > 0.0:
                agg[a] += w
        return dict(agg), len(votes)

    def _classical_scores(self, family: str, obs: Dict[str, Any], primitives: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[Any, float]:
        """
        Minimal classical baselines:
          - bandit: empirical means via primitive bandit_stats (else internal)
          - renewal: predict-last
          - maze: greedy-to-goal (non-improving moves get a small floor)
        """
        if family == "bandit":
            n = int(obs.get("n_arms", 2))
            bs = primitives.get("bandit_stats")
            if bs is not None and all(hasattr(bs, k) for k in ("ensure","means","counts")):
                try:
                    bs.ensure(n)
                    means = list(bs.means[:n])
                except Exception:
                    self._ensure_arms(n); means = list(self._means[:n])
            else:
                self._ensure_arms(n); means = list(self._means[:n])
            if any(means):
                lo, hi = min(means), max(means)
                rng = (hi - lo) if (hi > lo) else 1.0
                return {i: (means[i]-lo)/rng for i in range(n)}
            return {i: 0.0 for i in range(n)}

        if family == "renewal":
            a = int(obs.get("obs", 0))
            return {a: 1.0}

        if family == "maze":
            pos = obs.get("pos"); goal = obs.get("goal")
            H = obs.get("height"); W = obs.get("width"); grid = obs.get("grid")

            if not (isinstance(pos,(list,tuple)) and isinstance(goal,(list,tuple))):
                print("[CLASSIC] missing pos/goal -> no classical scores")
                return {}

            pr,pc = int(pos[0]), int(pos[1]); gr,gc = int(goal[0]), int(goal[1])
            dirs = ("UP","DOWN","LEFT","RIGHT")
            deltas = {"UP":(-1,0),"DOWN":(1,0),"LEFT":(0,-1),"RIGHT":(0,1)}

            def inb(r,c):
                if H is None or W is None: return True
                try: return 0 <= r < int(H) and 0 <= c < int(W)
                except Exception: return True

            def free(r,c):
                if not inb(r,c): return False
                if grid is None: return True
                try: return int(grid[r][c]) == 0
                except Exception: return True

            print(f"[CLASSIC] pos={ (pr,pc) } goal={ (gr,gc) } HxW={H}x{W} grid_is_list={ isinstance(grid, list) }")

            d0 = abs(pr-gr)+abs(pc-gc)
            scores: Dict[str, float] = {}

            for d,(dr,dc) in deltas.items():
                nr, nc = pr+dr, pc+dc
                ok = free(nr,nc)
                cell = None
                if isinstance(grid, list) and H is not None and W is not None and 0 <= nr < int(H) and 0 <= nc < int(W):
                    try:
                        cell = int(grid[nr][nc])
                    except Exception:
                        cell = "?"

                print(f"[CLASSIC] dir={d} -> next={(nr,nc)} free={ok} cell={cell}")

                if not ok:
                    continue

                d1 = abs(nr-gr)+abs(nc-gc)
                improve = d0 - d1
                scores[d] = 1.0 if (improve > 0.0) else 0.2

            print("[CLASSIC] scores=", scores)
            return scores

        return {}

    # ----------------- hooks -----------------
    def update(
        self,
        observation: Dict[str, Any],
        primitives: Dict[str, Any],
        header: Any,
        feedback: Optional[Dict[str, Any]],
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        fam = str(observation.get("family", "")).lower()

        # fallback bandit stats update only when no primitive
        if fam == "bandit" and isinstance(feedback, dict):
            a = feedback.get("action", None)
            r = feedback.get("reward", None)
            n_arms = int(observation.get("n_arms", 2))
            bs = primitives.get("bandit_stats")
            if isinstance(a, int) and isinstance(r, (int, float)):
                if bs is not None and hasattr(bs, "update"):
                    try:
                        bs.update(int(a), float(r), n_arms=n_arms)
                    except Exception:
                        self._ensure_arms(n_arms)
                        self._counts[a] += 1
                        n = max(1, self._counts[a])
                        self._means[a] += (float(r) - self._means[a]) / float(n)
                else:
                    self._ensure_arms(n_arms)
                    self._counts[a] += 1
                    n = max(1, self._counts[a])
                    self._means[a] += (float(r) - self._means[a]) / float(n)
        return {}

    def step(
        self,
        observation: Dict[str, Any],
        primitives: Dict[str, Any],
        header: Any,
        feedback: Optional[Dict[str, Any]],
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            family = str(observation.get("family", "")).lower()
            actions = observation.get("action_space") or self._default_action_space(family, observation)

            # --- weights ---
            if self.co_weight_override is not None:
                co_w = float(max(0.0, min(1.0, self.co_weight_override)))
            else:
                try:
                    co_w = float(getattr(header, "state", {}).get("co_weight", 1.0))
                except Exception:
                    co_w = 1.0
            if self.blend_mode == "co_only":
                co_w = 1.0
            elif self.blend_mode == "classic_only":
                co_w = 0.0
            classic_w = 1.0 - co_w

            # --- CO path (bus, then translator, then fuse) ---
            co_sources: List[str] = []
            bus_scores, n_votes = ({}, 0)
            if self.prefer_bus:
                bus_scores, n_votes = self._bus_scores(primitives, family)
                if bus_scores:
                    co_sources.append("bus")

            trans_scores = {}
            translator_mask: set = set()
            if self.use_translator:
                translator = get_translator_for_family(family)
                if translator is not None:
                    tcfg = {
                        "eps": self.eps,
                        "maze_explore": self._maze_explore,
                        "k": self.k,
                    }
                    try:
                        trans_scores, translator_mask, _info = translator(observation, header, primitives, {}, tcfg)
                    except Exception:
                        trans_scores, translator_mask = {}, set()
                    if trans_scores:
                        co_sources.append("translator")

            co_scores = {}
            parts = []
            if bus_scores:   parts.append(bus_scores)
            if trans_scores: parts.append(trans_scores)
            if parts:
                co_scores = self._fuser.fuse(parts)
                co_scores = normalize_scores(co_scores)
            # apply translator mask to CO scores (if any)
            for a in list(co_scores.keys()):
                if a in translator_mask:
                    co_scores.pop(a, None)

            

            # --- classical path ---
            classical = self._classical_scores(family, observation, primitives)
            if classical:
                classical = normalize_scores(classical)
                co_sources.append("classical")  # we will blend it (possibly with weight 0)

            # --- assemble final scores ---
            domain = list(actions) if actions else list(set(list(co_scores.keys()) + list(classical.keys())))
            final_scores: Dict[Any, float] = {}
            if domain:
                for a in domain:
                    cs = co_scores.get(a, 0.0)
                    ks = classical.get(a, 0.0)
                    final_scores[a] = co_w * cs + classic_w * ks
                
            if final_scores:
                best = max(final_scores, key=final_scores.get)
                return {
                    "action": best,
                    "co_policy": f"{family}:blend(co={co_w:.2f})",
                    "co_bus_votes": int(n_votes),
                    "co_weight": float(co_w),
                    "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                    "co_sources": co_sources,
                    "head_eps": float(self.eps),
                    "head_ngram_order": int(self.k),
                }

            # -------- HEURISTIC FALLBACKS --------------------
            if family == "bandit":
                n_arms = int(observation.get("n_arms", 2))
                self._ensure_arms(n_arms)
                for i in range(n_arms):
                    if self._counts[i] == 0:
                        return {"action": i, "co_policy": "bandit:fallback_roundrobin",
                                "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_weight": float(co_w), "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                                "co_sources": ["fallback"], "head_eps": float(self.eps), "head_ngram_order": int(self.k)}
                if self.rng.random() < self.eps:
                    a = self.rng.randrange(n_arms)
                else:
                    a = max(range(n_arms), key=lambda j: self._means[j])
                return {"action": a, "co_policy": "bandit:fallback_egreedy",
                        "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_weight": float(co_w), "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                        "co_sources": ["fallback"], "head_eps": float(self.eps), "head_ngram_order": int(self.k)}

            if family == "renewal":
                a = int(observation.get("obs", 0))
                return {"action": a, "co_policy": "renewal:fallback_predict_last",
                        "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_weight": float(co_w), "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                        "co_sources": ["fallback"], "head_eps": float(self.eps), "head_ngram_order": int(self.k)}

            if family == "maze":
                pos = observation.get("pos"); goal = observation.get("goal")
                if isinstance(pos, (list, tuple)) and isinstance(goal, (list, tuple)):
                    pr, pc = int(pos[0]), int(pos[1])
                    gr, gc = int(goal[0]), int(goal[1])
                    dirs = ("UP", "DOWN", "LEFT", "RIGHT")
                    deltas = {"UP": (-1, 0), "DOWN": (1, 0), "LEFT": (0, -1), "RIGHT": (0, 1)}
                    best = None; best_improve = -1e9
                    d0 = abs(pr - gr) + abs(pc - gc)
                    for d in dirs:
                        dr, dc = deltas[d]
                        d1 = abs((pr + dr) - gr) + abs((pc + dc) - gc)
                        improve = d0 - d1
                        if improve > best_improve:
                            best_improve = improve
                            best = d
                    return {"action": best or "RIGHT", "co_policy": "maze:fallback_greedy",
                            "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_weight": float(co_w), "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                            "co_sources": ["fallback"], "head_eps": float(self.eps), "head_ngram_order": int(self.k)}

            # Unknown family or no choice available
            if actions:
                return {"action": actions[0], "co_policy": "fallback:any",
                        "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_weight": float(co_w), "classic_weight": float(classic_w),
                        "co_sources": ["fallback"], "head_eps": float(self.eps), "head_ngram_order": int(self.k)}
            return {}

        except Exception:
            # Ultra-robust maze fallback so the runner never stalls
            fam = str(observation.get("family","")).lower()
            if fam == "maze":
                pos = observation.get("pos"); goal = observation.get("goal")
                if isinstance(pos,(list,tuple)) and isinstance(goal,(list,tuple)):
                    pr, pc = int(pos[0]), int(pos[1]); gr, gc = int(goal[0]), int(goal[1])
                    dirs = ("UP","DOWN","LEFT","RIGHT")
                    deltas = {"UP":(-1,0),"DOWN":(1,0),"LEFT":(0,-1),"RIGHT":(0,1)}
                    best = None; best_improve = -1e9
                    d0 = abs(pr-gr)+abs(pc-gc)
                    for d in dirs:
                        dr,dc = deltas[d]
                        d1 = abs(pr+dr-gr)+abs(pc+dc-gc)
                        imp = d0 - d1
                        if imp > best_improve:
                            best_improve, best = imp, d
                    return {"action": best or "RIGHT", "co_policy": "maze:fallback_greedy", "co_bus_votes": 0,
                            "co_sources": ["fallback"]}
            # unknown family: pick anything
            actions = observation.get("action_space") or []
            return {"action": (actions[0] if actions else None), "co_policy": "fallback:any",
                    "co_bus_votes": 0, "co_sources": ["fallback"]}

    def run_update(
        self,
        elements: list,
        primitives: dict,
        header: any,
        observation: dict,
        feedback: dict | None,
    ) -> dict:
        """Learning-only pass; no ActionHead.step, no return of an action."""
        out: dict = {}
        try:
            hrec = header.update(observation)
            if isinstance(hrec, dict):
                out.update(hrec)
        except Exception:
            pass

        for e in elements:
            # skip ActionHead entirely on update pass
            if e.__class__.__name__.lower().endswith("actionhead"):
                continue

            if hasattr(e, "update"):
                try:
                    u = e.update(observation, primitives, header, feedback)
                    if isinstance(u, dict) and u:
                        out.update(u)
                except Exception:
                    pass

            if hasattr(e, "step"):
                try:
                    s = e.step(observation, primitives, header, feedback)
                    if isinstance(s, dict) and s:
                        out.update(s)
                except Exception:
                    pass

            if hasattr(e, "metrics"):
                try:
                    m = e.metrics()
                    if isinstance(m, dict) and m:
                        out.update(m)
                except Exception:
                    pass

        return out

    def metrics(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "head_eps": float(self.eps),
            "head_ngram_order": int(self.k),
        }

Co — Master Guide (v1
CO — Master Guide (v1.0)

Purpose
A complete, self‑contained specification of Change Ontology (CO) logic and mathematics: motivations → definitions → formulas with symbol legends → algorithms → how pieces interlock. It’s written so a reader without access to AI‑12..18/FND‑0 can learn everything that appears there. Classical mathematics is rigorously embedded as a special case.

0) Quick Orientation & Label Map

AI‑13 dashboard ⇄ this guide

AI‑13 ID	Name	Tag here
A	History‑Adaptive Gauge	[HAQ]
B	Gödel‑hole detection + variable creation	[HOLE], [VB]
C	Identity as bend‑equivalence	[ID~τ], [D], [Δ]
D	Subjective metric warp	[WARP], [AQ]
E	Compressibility & attractor robustness	[κ/MDL], [Γ]
F	Global Invariants Layer (router)	[GIL], [HDR:CS/ID/SSI]
G	Density/precision knob	[DENSITY], [Σ]
H	Breadth–Depth scheduler	[BDSCHED]
I	Change‑native operators	[OPS⊕⊗], [ALG:min,+]

Aliases used in chats: GHVC ≡ [HOLE]+[VB]; Classical recovery gate ≡ [HDR:CS]; Density knob ≡ [DENSITY]/[Σ]; Change‑operators ≡ [OPS⊕⊗]; “Meta‑flip/OPS‑first” is enforced by [GIL].

1) Notation & Symbols

Paths / histories: π, ρ. Eventlets (minimally distinguishable occurrences): e. Concatenation: π·ρ.

Bend (local rewrite) of subpath σ→σ' with non‑negative cost C(σ⇒σ').

Local bend cost family (insert/delete/substitute/warp/curvature): Δ.

Bend distance (Lawvere metric): D(π,π') = inf total bend cost turning π→π'.

Tolerance / identity radius: τ, ε ≥ 0. Identity “up to τ”: π ~_τ π' ⇔ D(π,π') ≤ τ.

Gauge / attention field: A; warped costs: C_A = C − α A (with positivity guard so costs stay ≥0).

Holonomy (order effect): H (e.g., difference AB vs BA loop scores).

MDL (two‑part code length): κ (shorter is better); ΔMDL < 0 means improvement.

Robustness gap (min bend to leave an attractor): Γ(A).

Spread number (CO number): x = (μ, b, d) with central value μ, breadth spread b, depth/precision spread d.

Operators: choice ⊕ (min), sequence ⊗ (min‑plus convolution), merge‑within‑tolerance ⊕_ε, composition ⊗_ε, residuation ⇒, conditioning |C, closure cl_ε, coarse‑grain/quotient Π_ε.

Temporal: next X_ε, eventually F_{≤k,ε}, always G_ε, until U_ε.

Headers/regimes: [HDR:CS] (classical slice), [HDR:ID] (subject‑local), [HDR:SSI] (objective), router [GIL].

2) First Principles (Derivation Chain)

P0. Immediate datum (succession). There are minimally distinguishable “nows” and admissible transitions e→e'.

P1. Paths. A path π = e₁ e₂ … e_n respects admissibility.

P2. Bend & cost. A bend replaces a contiguous subpath; costs add under concatenation; zero cost for identity.

P3. Bend distance. D(π,π') = inf over bend sequences of the summed costs. Properties: nonnegativity, identity of indiscernibles at τ=0, triangle, reparam‑invariance; coarse‑grain stability is conjectured and tested (see §15 Open Proofs).

P4. Tolerance & identity. π ~_τ π' iff D(π,π') ≤ τ. Tolerance τ must be cited—identity is never absolute off the classical slice.

P5. Gauge (attention). Attention A warps perceived costs: C_A = C − α A. A updates by surprise/utility (HAQ, §8). This yields path‑dependence off‑slice (holonomy H).

These primitives force an idempotent semiring on path costs: choice = min, sequence = + (the min‑plus or tropical “dioid”).

3) CO‑Logic (Truth as Least Bend Budget)

Semantics. Truth of a statement φ on a realized path π is the least bend budget to make φ hold:

⟦φ⟧_π := inf over π' that satisfy φ of D(π,π') ∈ [0, ∞].

“Smaller” means “truer”. With the Lawvere order (≥ as ≤‑truth), ([0,∞], ⊗=+, ∨=min, ∧=max, ⇒=truncated subtraction) is a commutative quantale / complete residuated lattice.

Connectives

Disjunction: a ∨ b = min(a,b) (easiest sufficient path).

Conjunction: a ∧ b = max(a,b) (hardest simultaneous requirement).

Sequential “and‑then”: a ⊗ b = a + b (budgets add).

Implication (residuation): a ⇒ b = max(0, b − a) with the residuation law a⊗c ≤ b ⇔ c ≤ (a⇒b).

Quantifiers: ∃x := inf_x , ∀x := sup_x .

Temporal operators under tolerance

Next X_ε P : there exists a one‑step bend ≤ ε to a state satisfying P.

Eventually F_{≤k,ε} P : within k steps, extra cost ≤ ε to reach P.

Always G_ε P : all continuations stay ε‑reidentifiable with P.

Until P U_ε Q : along the path, P holds (within ε) until (within ε) Q holds.

Slices unify logics
Restricting the truth‑value scale recovers: Boolean ({0,∞}), fuzzy ([0,1] with monotone rescaling), probabilistic (negative log‑likelihood as costs), modal/temporal (reachability under ε).

4) CO‑Math (Numbers as Spreads)

A spread encodes value + uncertainty in two native CO directions:

x = (μ, b, d) ∈ ℝ × [0,∞)^2

μ: central scalar (report if forced to a point).

b (breadth): variability across alternate continuations.

d (depth): representation precision (rounding/compute tolerance).

Order: x ⪯ y iff μ_x≤μ_y, b_x≤b_y, d_x≤d_y.

Addition (Minkowski‑style):
x ⊞ y = (μ_x+μ_y, b_x+b_y, d_x+d_y).

Multiplication (first‑order safe propagation):
x ⊠ y = (μ_x μ_y, |μ_x| b_y + |μ_y| b_x + b_x b_y, |μ_x| d_y + |μ_y| d_x + d_x d_y).

Residuation (“division”): the tightest h with x⊠h ⪯ z. First‑order Taylor rules give safe formulas; exact inverses need not exist (spreads don’t cancel).
Embedding of reals: x ↦ (x,0,0) is a semiring monomorphism; setting b=d=0 recovers classical +, ·.

Structure: an ordered commutative semiring with residuation; not a ring (additive inverses would break robustness).

5) Path Algebra & Operators (CO‑native)

Let cost kernels f,g : U×U→[0,∞].

Choice (⊕): (f ⊕ g)(u,v) = min{ f(u,v), g(u,v) }. Idempotent, commutative.

Sequence (⊗) (min‑plus convolution): (f ⊗ g)(u,v) = min_w { f(u,w) + g(w,v) }. Associative; distributes over ⊕.

Residuation (⇒): largest h with f⊗h ≤ d; scalar form a⇒b = max(0, b−a).

Conditioning (|C): forbid bends leaving C (cost = +∞ outside C).

Closure (cl_ε): cl_ε(S) = { π : D(π,S) ≤ ε } (Kuratowski laws).

Coarse‑grain/quotient (Π_ε): collapse to classes under ~_ε.

Merge within tolerance (⊕_ε): medoid/prototype merge of k‑grams under D ≤ ε; idempotent, approx‑associative.

Composition (⊗_ε): overlap‑aware concatenation removing best ε‑match; quasi‑associative on histories.

Identity, holonomy, classical slice

[ID~τ]: identity is equivalence under bend distance ≤ τ.

[H]: order‑effects measured by AB vs BA loops; H→0 on [HDR:CS].

[HDR:CS] (classical): τ=0, A≡0, spreads=0, D→D_{C0}.

6) Headers / Regimes / Router

[HDR:CS] Classical slice — enforce H ≈ 0 and baseline parity before claiming world invariants.

[HDR:ID] Subject‑local — thresholds encode the subject‑instrument (UX/clinical).

[HDR:SSI] Objective mode — require refinement/gauge invariance across agents.

[GIL] Global Invariants Layer — probes (volatility, repeat‑subpaths, holonomy, ΔMDL) to route to CS vs CO; tags outputs with regime metadata (scale, ε, h, τ, A, slice_flag).

7) Metrics & Criteria

[κ/MDL] Two‑part code length (model + residual). Prefer ΔMDL < 0.

[Γ] Robustness gap: minimal bend to exit attractor (higher is safer).

[J‑criterion]: J1 reportability; J2 order‑sensitivity; J3 compressibility; J4 control leverage.

[MRAI] Intersubject agreement: mutual prediction + invariant match (up to gauge) + order‑alignment + control concordance.

[Loopiness L]: cycles/Betti‑1/return‑prob@t; informs [BDSCHED].

8) Elements (from primitives)

[HAQ] History‑Adaptive Gauge
Definition. Habit state A updates by surprise vs expected gain (α fast / β slow / leak). Perceived costs C_A = C − α A.
Role. Warps metric, shapes attractors, interacts with variable‑birth and exploration.

[VB] Variable‑Birth
Definition. Accept a new latent z_k only if: (i) residual EMA persistently high and (ii) ΔMDL ≤ −γ and (iii) prediction error non‑increasing for T steps; enforce cooldown C.
Why. Prevent gratuitous variables; encode true new structure.

[HOLE] Gödel‑hole (operational)
Definition. Persistent residuals + non‑zero holonomy that survive resequencing/ε,h retuning indicate a representational impasse; resolve via ladder: resequence → retune Σ (ε,h) → update gauge A → attempt [VB].

[BDSCHED] Breadth–Depth scheduler
Definition. Adapt p(breadth) by loopiness L and regret; favor BFS in high‑loop graphs (small spectral gap γ), DFS in tree‑like regimes.

[WARP] Subjective metric warp
Definition. A gauge‑dependent equivalence that stabilizes motifs even when base rules are unchanged (e.g., CA motifs). Independent criterion from HAQ’s planner.

9) OPS (Objective Problem Shape)

[OPS‑Maze]
Data: graph G=(V,E), metric d_G, spectral gap γ, potential Φ, automorphisms Aut(G).
Claims reported only after [HDR:CS] gate: H→0, baseline parity.

[OPS‑Bandit]
Data: arms {ν_i}, gaps Δ_i, KL table, corruption model.

[OPS‑Renewal]
Data: inter‑arrival law class, hazard h(t), tail index α, renewal vs Hawkes; stationarity.

[OPS pipeline] normalize → fit world model → compute invariants → refinement/gauge invariance → [HDR:CS] gate → ablations.

10) Probability (CO view)

Events are classes in the quotient P/~_ε.

CO probability of template T is its re‑identification frequency:
E_ε[1_T] = lim_{n→∞} (1/n) Σ_{t≤n} 1(π_t ~_ε T).

LLN (sketch): on the coarse chain induced by ~_ε, ergodicity ⇒ time averages converge to stationary expectations.

11) Ethics & Governance

[ISA] Informed Sequence Autonomy — sequence shaping only with inspect/reset gauge, disclosure, and consent.

[Dynamic‑Category Rights] — on [VB] accept: notice, audit log, fairness test, rollback if disparity>δ; SLA (e.g., 24h/7d).

12) Algorithms (Pseudocode)

12.1 [HAQ] loop

state A  # habit/gauge
for t = 1..T:
    # perception
    cost = C - alpha * A  # positivity guard enforced
    action = Planner(cost)
    obs, err = step(action)


    # updates
    A = (1 - beta) * A + alpha_fast * Surprise(err) - leak * A

12.2 [VB] acceptor

if residual_ema > theta_res and H > theta_H:
    propose z_new = learn_latent()
    if delta_MDL(z_new) <= -gamma and err_nonincreasing(T_window):
        if cooldown_ok(C): accept(z_new)

12.3 Holonomy assay [H]

score_AB = probe(sequence=A_then_B)
score_BA = probe(sequence=B_then_A)
H = norm(score_AB - score_BA)

12.4 OPS pipeline

normalize(data)
M_T = fit_world_model(data)
inv = compute_invariants(M_T)
check_refinement_invariance(inv)
check_gauge_invariance(inv)
assert classical_gate_passed(H ~ 0 and perf ≈ baseline)
run_ablations()
13) Engineering Patterns

[CO‑IR] Intermediate record: {obs, event, state, A, residual EMA, ΔMDL, invariants, action, regime tags}.

Combinators: pipeline (∘), overlay (⊕), product (⊗), header/gate (▷), lens. Each module declares capability contracts: policy/update/probe/ops/slice_ok.

Adapters (Maze/Bandit/Renewal) export classical D_{C0} & OPS with confidence intervals.

Smuggling detector: flag if a module ignores τ/A, or exhibits H≈0 off CS, or OPS changes across ε,h sweeps/agents.

14) Classical Embedding (Consistency)

Set ε=0, A≡0, spreads=0. Then: CO‑logic → Boolean logic; CO‑numbers → (ℝ,+,·); CO‑sets/maps/bijections reduce to classical; operators collapse to identities or standard forms. This is a full and faithful embedding of classical math inside CO.

15) Programs & Open Proofs (what remains to formalize)

[D‑A5] Coarse‑grain stability of D (proof; empirical evidence is positive).

CO‑measure (Choquet‑style integral coherent with spreads) and LLN/CLT on quotient chains.

CO‑calculus: chain rule & Grönwall bounds in cost geometry; subgradient dynamics for learning under bend costs.

Category‑theoretic unification: CO‑spaces as Lawvere‑quantale enriched; HAQ as approximate idempotent monad.

16) Quick Lookup (tags → formulas → where used)

[ID~τ]: π~_τπ' iff D(π,π') ≤ τ. Used by: [VB], [OPS], [MRAI].

[H]: AB vs BA difference; used by [HOLE], [HDR:CS] gate.

[⊗]: (f⊗g)(u,v) = min_w f(u,w) + g(w,v) in planners/temporal logic.

[⇒]: scalar a⇒b = max(0, b−a) ; kernel residuation is right division.

[E_ε[1_T]]: re‑ID frequency; probabilities as option frequencies.

[Γ]: min bend to exit attractor; monitor under [W_A].

[BDSCHED]: adapt p(breadth) by L, regret; choose DFS/BFS by evidence.

Co — Max‑clarity, Ops‑first (derivation • Philosophy • Formulas • Algorithms • Tests) V0.1
CO — Max‑Clarity, OPS‑First (Derivation • Philosophy • Formulas • Algorithms • Tests)

Purpose. A single, gap‑free document that gathers everything we’ve developed across AI‑12…18 + FND‑0: stepwise derivation, philosophical motivations, a symbol glossary (no undefined symbols), formal statements with status labels, runnable pseudocode, OPS (Objective Problem Shape) cards, assays/falsifiers, ethics hooks, and open items. OPS‑first: World/Task regularities (Objective Problem Shape, OPS) are the primary claim targets. Subjects/agents are instruments (meters) unless the subject is the mechanism of interest.

4) Algorithms (pseudocode; runnable spec)
4.1 HAQ loop (gauge update with two timescales)
for t in 1..T:
  x_t = observe()
  y_t = policy(x_t, A)                    # action under current gauge
  r_t, loss_t = environment(y_t)
  # gauge update
  A.alpha = decay(A.alpha); A.beta = decay(A.beta)
  A = A + A.alpha * grad_fast(x_t, y_t, r_t)
        + A.beta  * grad_slow(A)
        - leak * A
  residual_ema = EMA(residual_ema, loss_t, W)
  if residual_ema >= θ_on and cooldown == 0:
      add_variable()
      cooldown = C
  if cooldown > 0 and residual_ema <= θ_off:
      cooldown -= 1
4.2 Variable‑birth (MDL‑guarded)
function add_variable():
  propose new latent z_k
  fit minimal params on window W
  if MDL_total <= (1-γ) * MDL_prev and error_nonincreasing(200):
      accept z_k
  else:
      reject
4.3 Bend‑distance (edit‑path DP sketch)
function D(pi, pi'):
  return min_cost_edit(pi, pi', local_cost=Δ,
                       constraints=[locality, monotone_refinement])
4.4 Holonomy assay
s0 = snapshot()
for phase in [A, B, A]:
  run_phase(phase, gauge=AQ)
H = norm(snapshot() - s0)
4.5 Classical slice check
set tau=0; A=0; spreads=0
assert performance(HAQ) ≈ performance(no_gauge) ≈ baseline_D_C0 within 1%
assert order_effects(HAQ) ~ 0
4.6 OPS discovery pipeline (agent‑agnostic)
INPUT: logs from agents {S_k} on task T
STEP 1: normalize time; set tau=0; remove gauge (A=0) where possible
STEP 2: fit world model M_T (maze graph; bandit arm family; renewal law)
STEP 3: compute invariants I_T (e.g., {G, d_G, γ, Φ} or {Δ, KL} or {h(t), α})
STEP 4: cross‑agent CI overlap on I_T
STEP 5: refinement stability vs ε,h sweeps
STEP 6: ablations (wrong/no‑gauge) → invariants unchanged
OUTPUT: OPS card + CIs + ablation table
4.7 Two‑subject agreement (MRAI)
for task in T:
  P = mutual_prediction_score(Sa, Sb)
  I = 1 - normalized_invariant_distance(Sa, Sb)
  A = order_effect_alignment(Sa, Sb)
  C = control_concordance(Sa, Sb)
  MRAI = wP*P + wI*I + wA*A + wC*C
agree = count(MRAI >= θ_agree) >= k

6) Assays & Falsifiers (checklist)
6.1 Immediate datum → SSI upgrade

Upgrade if: refinement stability, gauge robustness, intersubject coverage, predictive closure (MDL gain).

Fail if: event rate flat vs 
𝜀
,
